     <section class="gb-mb-6 nchp-faq-section" id="faq-section">
      <div class="gb-container">
       <p class="nchp-h1 gb-mb-2">
        Frequently asked questions
       </p>
       <div class="gb-row">
        <div class="gb-col gb-col-md-10 gb-col-lg-9 gb-col-xl-7">
         <div class="gb-mb-3">
          <div class="gb-collapse">
           <div class="gb-collapse__trigger" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-customhandler="homePage.faqDropdown" data-et-label="Why buy a domain name from Namecheap?">
            <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">
             Why buy a domain name from Namecheap?
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3">
            <p>
             Above all else, we strive to deliver outstanding customer experiences. When you buy a domain name from Namecheap, we guarantee it will be handed over to you with superior standards of service and support. Our primary goal is to build a customer-focused atmosphere filled with the happiest customers in the galaxy. The Namecheap guarantee is our mark of excellence.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gb-collapse">
           <div class="gb-collapse__trigger" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-customhandler="homePage.faqDropdown" data-et-label="Why is domain name registration required?">
            <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">
             Why is domain name registration required?
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3">
            <p>
             When you build a website, you want visitors to come and see what you've done. To get them there, you need a unique domain name that connects to your site's servers. Domain name registration is required to ensure that no one else in the world can claim ownership of your site's address and to make finding your website simple.
             <a data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - Link" data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-label="/domains/domain-name-search/" href="/domains/domain-name-search/">
              Find your one of a kind domain name.
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gb-collapse">
           <div class="gb-collapse__trigger" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-customhandler="homePage.faqDropdown" data-et-label="How does domain registration work?">
            <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">
             How does domain registration work?
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3">
            <p>
             Think of the name you want to register. The answer is typically your company or website name. It is best to keep your domain name short and easy to understand. Say it out loud, and make sure it sounds great. Next, search to see if it is available. If the name you desire is taken with the .com top-level domain, there are hundreds of others available. Finally, add the top choices to your cart and complete the domain registration.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gb-collapse">
           <div class="gb-collapse__trigger" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-customhandler="homePage.faqDropdown" data-et-label="What domains are available from Namecheap?">
            <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">
             What domains are available from Namecheap?
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3">
            <p>
             At Namecheap, you can register brand new domain names using hundreds of popular TLDs. In our Marketplace, you will find thousands of domain names that have already been registered but are now for sale. While .com domains are available, of course, you'll also see options using .net, .us, and many more.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gb-collapse">
           <div class="gb-collapse__trigger" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-customhandler="homePage.faqDropdown" data-et-label="Can you buy domain names and sell them?">
            <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">
             Can you buy domain names and sell them?
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3">
            <p>
             If you have purchased domain names that you no longer need, you can sell them through Namecheap. When you are ready to sell, you can list your domain in our
             <a data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - Link" data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-label="/domains/marketplace/buy-domains/" href="/domains/marketplace/buy-domains/">
              Marketplace
             </a>
             for a fixed price. We will add your domains to our searchable list, visited by thousands of people every day. When you buy domain names from Namecheap, we guarantee the best available support from managing, to selling, to renewals.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gb-collapse">
           <div class="gb-collapse__trigger" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-customhandler="homePage.faqDropdown" data-et-label="Whats the best way to find a cheap domain?">
            <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">
             Whats the best way to find a cheap domain?
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3">
            <p>
             Its all about knowing where to look. Weve gathered together our most popular
             <a data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - Link" data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-label="/promos/" href="/promos/">
              deals on one page
             </a>
             so you can easily find your perfect domain name, hosting, and more at affordable prices. Just take a look.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gb-collapse">
           <div class="gb-collapse__trigger" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-customhandler="homePage.faqDropdown" data-et-label="How do I choose the right domain registrar?">
            <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">
             How do I choose the right domain registrar?
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3">
            <p>
             While price is a big factor, there are also other areas to consider when
             <a data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - Link" data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-label="/blog/4-things-to-look-for-in-a-domain-registrar/" href="/blog/4-things-to-look-for-in-a-domain-registrar/">
              choosing the right domain registrar
             </a>
             . These include customer support, security, and effortless account management. All of which come as standard with Namecheap  alongside a great price, of course.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
